-- Estrutura da tabela `administrator_modules`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `administrator_modules`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `administrator_modules` (
  `idAdministrator` int NOT NULL,
  `idModule` int NOT NULL,
  `pView` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `pInsert` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `pUpdate` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `pDelete` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `updated` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idAdministrator`,`idModule`),
  KEY `idModule` (`idModule`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

  `idWorksheet` int DEFAULT NULL,

  `num` int NOT NULL,

  `updated` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

  KEY `idClient` (`idClient`),
  KEY `idWorksheet` (`idWorksheet`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=87 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estrutura da tabela `budget_version`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `budget_version`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `budget_version` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `idVersion` int NOT NULL,
  `idBudget` int NOT NULL,
  `nameSection` text COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `orderSection` int NOT NULL,
  `idProduct` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `orderProduct` int NOT NULL,
  `checkProduct` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `storageProduct` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `refProduct` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `nameProduct` varchar(250) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `amountProduct` int NOT NULL,
  `descriptionProduct` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci,
  `observationProduct` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci,
  `sizeProduct` varchar(250) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `valueProduct` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idBudget` (`idBudget`,`idProduct`),
  KEY `idProduct` (`idProduct`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1982 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estrutura da tabela `client`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `client`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `client` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `contact` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `nif` varchar(12) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `updated` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=22 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `product`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `product` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `reference` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `value` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `size` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `img` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci,
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `updated` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=21 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=46 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Restrições para despejos de tabelas
--

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `administrator_logs`
--
ALTER TABLE `administrator_logs`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `administrator_logs_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`idAdministrator`) REFERENCES `administrator` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `administrator_modules`
--
ALTER TABLE `administrator_modules`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `administrator_modules_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`idModule`) REFERENCES `modules` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `budget`
--
ALTER TABLE `budget`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`idClient`) REFERENCES `client` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`idWorksheet`) REFERENCES `worksheet` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `budget_sections_products`
--
ALTER TABLE `budget_sections_products`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_sections_products_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`idBudget`) REFERENCES `budget` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_sections_products_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`idProduct`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `budget_version`
--
ALTER TABLE `budget_version`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_version_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`idBudget`) REFERENCES `budget` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `budget_version_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`idProduct`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `product_stock`
--
ALTER TABLE `product_stock`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `product_stock_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`idProduct`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

--
-- Limitadores para a tabela `worksheet`
--
ALTER TABLE `worksheet`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `worksheet_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`idClient`) REFERENCES `client` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;
